ToolTipHelp.img\Game\Button\SkillAlert\hyper\DescThese powerful skills become available after Lv. 140. \n\n#cPassive Hyper Skills# boosts your existing skills in different ways. You'll gain 1 SP at Levels 140, 160, 180, 190, and 200. \n\n#cActive Hyper Skills# are powerful active skills. A new one is unlocked at Levels 150, 170, and 200. Buff Hyper Skills are not affected by effects that would decrease cooldown and effects that would increase their duration.These powerful skills become available after Lv. 140. \n\n#cPassive Hyper Skills# boosts your existing skills in different ways.
